<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July 25, 2007,
Apple&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Apple&#148;) issued a press release regarding Apple&#146;s financial
results for its third fiscal quarter ended June 30, 2007 and a related data
sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1
and a copy of the related data sheet is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information contained
in this Current Report shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or
incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as
amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by
specific reference in such a filing.</font></p>

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports Third Quarter Results</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Record June Quarter Revenue and Profit</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mac Sales Set New Record</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;July 25, 2007&#151;Apple&#174; today
announced financial results for its fiscal 2007 third quarter ended June 30,
2007. The Company posted revenue of $5.41 billion and net quarterly profit of
$818 million, or $.92 per diluted share. These results compare to revenue of
$4.37 billion and net quarterly profit of $472 million, or $.54 per diluted
share, in the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 36.9 percent, up from 30.3
percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for 40 percent
of the quarter&#146;s revenue.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple
shipped 1,764,000 Macintosh&#174; computers, representing 33 percent growth over the
year-ago quarter and exceeding the previous company record for quarterly Mac&#174;
shipments by over 150,000. The Company also sold 9,815,000 iPods during the
quarter, representing 21 percent growth over the year-ago quarter.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We&#146;re
thrilled to report the highest June quarter revenue and profit in Apple&#146;s
history, along with the highest quarterly Mac sales ever,&#148; said Steve Jobs,
Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;iPhone is off to a great start&#151;we hope to sell our one-millionth
iPhone by the end of its first full quarter of sales&#151;and our new product
pipeline is very strong.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are
very pleased to report strong financial results including cash flow from
operations exceeding $1.2 billion for the quarter,&#148; said Peter Oppenheimer,
Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking ahead to the fourth fiscal quarter of 2007, we expect
revenue of about $5.7 billion and earnings per diluted share of about $.65.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple
will provide live streaming of its Q3 2007 financial results conference call
utilizing QuickTime&#174;, Apple&#146;s standards-based technology for live and on-demand
audio and video streaming. The live webcast will begin at 2:00 p.m. PDT on
Wednesday, July 25, 2007 at www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq307/ and will
also be available for replay. The QuickTime player is available free for
Macintosh and Windows users at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>

<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\205222156361_D11848_2273243\20193-1-kg.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Jul 24 22:22 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">This
press release contains forward-looking statements about the Company&#146;s estimated
revenue, iPhone&#153; sales and earnings per share. These statements involve risks
and uncertainties, and actual results may differ. Risks and uncertainties
include potential litigation and government enforcement actions that may result
from the matters investigated by the special committee of the board of
directors and the restatement of the Company&#146;s consolidated financial
statements; unfavorable results of legal proceedings; the effect of competitive
and economic factors, and the Company&#146;s reaction to those factors, on consumer
and business buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products; war,
terrorism, public health issues, and other circumstances that could disrupt
supply, delivery, or demand of products; continued competitive pressures in the
marketplace; the Company&#146;s reliance on a sole U.S. service provider for iPhone;
the continued availability on acceptable terms of certain components and
services essential to the Company&#146;s business currently obtained by the Company
from sole or limited sources; the ability of the Company to deliver to the
marketplace and stimulate customer demand for new programs, products, and
technological innovations on a timely basis; the effect that product
transitions, changes in product pricing or mix, and/or increases in component
costs could have on the Company&#146;s gross margin; the effect that product quality
problems could have on the Company&#146;s sales and operating profits; the inventory
risk associated with the Company&#146;s need to order or commit to order product
components in advance of customer orders; the effect that the Company&#146;s
dependency on manufacturing and logistics services provided by third parties
may have on the quality, quantity or cost of products manufactured or services
rendered; the Company&#146;s dependency on the performance of distributors and other
resellers of the Company&#146;s products; the Company&#146;s reliance on the availability
of third-party digital content; and the potential impact of a finding that the
Company has infringed on the intellectual property rights of others. More
information on potential factors that could affect the Company&#146;s financial
results is included from time to time in the Company&#146;s public reports filed
with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended
September 30, 2006, its Forms 10-Q for the quarters ended December 30, 2006 and
March 31, 2007, and its Form 10-Q for the quarter ended June 30, 2007 to be
filed with the SEC. The Company assumes no obligation to update any
forward-looking statements or information, which speak as of their respective
dates.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple
ignited the personal computer revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and
reinvented the personal computer in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Today, Apple
continues to lead the industry in innovation with its award-winning computers,
OS X operating system and iLife and professional applications. Apple is also
spearheading the digital media revolution with its iPod portable music and
video players and iTunes online store, and has entered the mobile phone market
this year with its revolutionary iPhone.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">In the third quarter of fiscal 2007, the Company
revised the way it measures the Retail Segment&#146;s operating results to a manner
that is generally consistent with the Company&#146;s other operating segments. Prior
period results have been reclassified to reflect this change to the Retail
Segment&#146;s operating results along with the corresponding offsets to the other
operating segments.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Other Segments include Asia Pacific and FileMaker.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Includes iMac, eMac, Mac mini, Mac Pro, PowerMac and
Xserve product lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Includes MacBook, iBook, MacBook Pro and PowerBook
product lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Consists of iTunes Store sales, iPod services, and
Apple-branded and third-party iPod accessories.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.0pt;">Consists of iPhones and Apple-branded and
